these and passes them to the update function.\\n+pub const Event = union(enum) {\\n+    /// Keyboard input event.\\n+    key: Key,\\n+\\n+    /// Mouse input event.\\n+    mouse: Mouse,\\n+\\n+    /// Terminal resize event.\\n+    resize: Size,\\n+\\n+    /// Timer tick event (for animations, polling).\\n+    tick: void,\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Keyboard event with key code and modifier state.\\n+pub const Key = struct {\\n+    code: KeyCode,\\n+    modifiers: Modifiers = .{},\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Key codes for keyboard input.\\n+/// Covers standard terminal key sequences.\\n+pub const KeyCode = union(enum) {\\n+    /// Unicode codepoint for printable characters.\\n+    char: u21,\\n+\\n+    /// Enter/Return key.\\n+    enter: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Tab key.\\n+    tab: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Shift+Tab (backtab).\\n+    backtab: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Backspace key.\\n+    backspace: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Escape key.\\n+    escape: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Arrow keys.\\n+    up: void,\\n+    down: void,\\n+    left: void,\\n+    right: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Navigation keys.\\n+    home: void,\\n+    end: void,\\n+    page_up: void,\\n+    page_down: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Edit keys.\\n+    insert: void,\\n+    delete: void,\\n+\\n+    /// Function keys (1-12).\\n+    f: u8,\\n+\\n+    /// Create a char KeyCode from a Unicode codepoint.\\n+    pub fn fromChar(c: u21) KeyCode {\\n+        return .{ .char = c };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a function key KeyCode (F1-F12).\\n+    /// Returns null if n is not in range 1-12.\\n+    pub fn fromF(n: u8) ?KeyCode {\\n+        if (n >= 1 and n <= 12) {\\n+            return .{ .f = n };\\n+        }\\n+        return null;\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if this is a printable character.\\n+    pub fn isChar(self: KeyCode) bool {\\n+        return self == .char;\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if this is an arrow key.\\n+    pub fn isArrow(self: KeyCode) bool {\\n+        return switch (self) {\\n+            .up, .down, .left, .right => true,\\n+            else => false,\\n+        };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if this is a navigation key (arrows, home, end, page up/down).\\n+    pub fn isNavigation(self: KeyCode) bool {\\n+        return switch (self) {\\n+            .up, .down, .left, .right, .home, .end, .page_up, .page_down => true,\\n+            else => false,\\n+        };\\n+    }\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Modifier key state (ctrl, alt, shift).\\n+pub const Modifiers = packed struct {\\n+    ctrl: bool = false,\\n+    alt: bool = false,\\n+    shift: bool = false,\\n+    _padding: u5 = 0,\\n+\\n+    /// No modifiers pressed.\\n+    pub const none: Modifiers = .{};\\n+\\n+    /// Create modifiers with only ctrl.\\n+    pub fn ctrl_only() Modifiers {\\n+        return .{ .ctrl = true };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create modifiers with only alt.\\n+    pub fn alt_only() Modifiers {\\n+        return .{ .alt = true };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create modifiers with only shift.\\n+    pub fn shift_only() Modifiers {\\n+        return .{ .shift = true };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if any modifier is pressed.\\n+    pub fn any(self: Modifiers) bool {\\n+        return self.ctrl or self.alt or self.shift;\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if no modifiers are pressed.\\n+    pub fn none_pressed(self: Modifiers) bool {\\n+        return !self.any();\\n+    }\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Mouse event with position, kind, and modifiers.\\n+pub const Mouse = struct {\\n+    x: u16,\\n+    y: u16,\\n+    kind: MouseKind,\\n+    modifiers: Modifiers = .{},\\n+\\n+    pub fn init(x: u16, y: u16, kind: MouseKind) Mouse {\\n+        return .{ .x = x, .y = y, .kind = kind };\\n+    }\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Mouse event kind.\\n+pub const MouseKind = enum {\\n+    down,\\n+    up,\\n+    drag,\\n+    move,\\n+    scroll_up,\\n+    scroll_down,\\n+\\n+    /// Check if this is a click event (down or up).\\n+    pub fn isClick(self: MouseKind) bool {\\n+        return self == .down or self == .up;\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if this is a scroll event.\\n+    pub fn isScroll(self: MouseKind) bool {\\n+        return self == .scroll_up or self == .scroll_down;\\n+    }\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Terminal size (from resize events).\\n+pub const Size = struct {\\n+    width: u16,\\n+    height: u16,\\n+\\n+    pub fn init(width: u16, height: u16) Size {\\n+        return .{ .width = width, .height = height };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Calculate area.\\n+    pub fn area(self: Size) u32 {\\n+        return @as(u32, self.width) * @as(u32, self.height);\\n+    }\\n+};\\n+\\n+// 100644\\nindex 0000000..ce7eb6f\\n--- /dev/null\\n+++ b/src/layout.zig\\n@@ -0,0 +1,203 @@\\n+// Layout types for zithril TUI framework\\n+// Constraint-based layout system inspired by ratatui\\n+\\n+const std = @import(\\\"std\\\");\\n+\\n+/// Direction for layout: how children are arranged.\\n+pub const Direction = enum {\\n+    horizontal,\\n+    vertical,\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Constraints describe how space should be allocated among layout children.\\n+///\\n+/// The constraint solver allocates space in this order:\\n+/// 1. Fixed constraints (length): Allocate exact requested size\\n+/// 2. Minimum constraints (min): Allocate at least requested size\\n+/// 3. Maximum constraints (max): Allocate at most requested size\\n+/// 4. Ratio constraints (ratio): Allocate fraction of total space\\n+/// 5. Flex constraints (flex): Distribute remaining space proportionally\\n+///\\n+/// When space is insufficient:\\n+/// - Fixed/min constraints take priority\\n+/// - Flex items shrink to zero before fixed items shrink\\n+/// - No negative sizes (saturating arithmetic)\\n+pub const Constraint = union(enum) {\\n+    /// Exactly n cells.\\n+    length: u16,\\n+\\n+    /// At least n cells.\\n+    min: u16,\\n+\\n+    /// At most n cells.\\n+    max: u16,\\n+\\n+    /// Fraction of available space (numerator, denominator).\\n+    /// Example: ratio(1, 3) means 1/3 of available space.\\n+    ratio: Ratio,\\n+\\n+    /// Proportional share (like CSS flex-grow).\\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(1) = 50/50 split\\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(2) = 33/67 split\\n+    flex: u16,\\n+\\n+    pub const Ratio = struct {\\n+        num: u16,\\n+        den: u16,\\n+    };\\n+\\n+    /// Create a length constraint (exactly n cells).\\n+    pub fn len(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .length = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a minimum constraint (at least n cells).\\n+    pub fn minSize(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .min = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a maximum constraint (at most n cells).\\n+    pub fn maxSize(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .max = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a ratio constraint (num/den of available space).\\n+    pub fn fractional(num: u16, den: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .ratio = .{ .num = num, .den = den } };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a flex constraint (proportional share).\\n+    pub fn flexible(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .flex = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Apply this constraint to resolve a concrete size given available space.\\n+    /// Returns the size this constraint requests, which may exceed available space.\\n+    /// The caller is responsible for ensuring the total doesn't exceed available.\\n+    pub fn apply(self: Constraint, available: u16) u16 {\\n+        return switch (self) {\\n+            .length => |n| n,\\n+            .min => |n| n,\\n+            .max => |n| @min(n, available),\\n+            .ratio => |r| blk: {\\n+                if (r.den == 0) break :blk 0;\\n+                const result = (@as(u32, available) * @as(u32, r.num)) / @as(u32, r.den);\\n+                break :blk @intCast(@min(result, available));\\n+            },\\n+            .flex => available,\\n+        };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if two constraints are equal.\\n+    pub fn eql(self: Constraint, other: Constraint) bool {\\n+        return switch (self) {\\n+            .length => |n| other == .length and other.length == n,\\n+            .min => |n| other == .min and other.min == n,\\n+            .max => |n| other == .max and other.max == n,\\n+            .ratio => |r| other == .ratio and other.ratio.num == r.num and other.ratio.den == r.den,\\n+            .flex => |n| other == .flex and other.flex == n,\\n+        };\\n+    }\\n+};\\n+\\n+// ============================================================\\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic functionality\\n+// ============================================================\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.len creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.len(10);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .length);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), c.length);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.minSize creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.minSize(20);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .min);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), c.min);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.maxSize creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(30);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .max);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.max);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.fractional creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 3);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .ratio);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), c.ratio.num);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 3), c.ratio.den);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.flexible creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.flexible(2);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .flex);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 2), c.flex);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Direction enum values\\\" {\\n+    try std.testing.expect(@intFromEnum(Direction.horizontal) != @intFromEnum(Direction.vertical));\\n+}\\n+\\n+// ============================================================\\n+// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Constraint application\\n+// ============================================================\\n+\\n+test \\\"behavior: Constraint length apply returns exact size\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.len(50);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(100));\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(30));\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"behavior: Constraint min apply returns minimum size\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.minSize(30);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(100));\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(20));\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"behavior: Constraint max apply caps at available\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(50);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(100));\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(30));\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"behavior: Constraint ratio apply calculates fraction\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 4);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 25), c.apply(100));\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(200));\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"behavior: Constraint ratio apply handles zero denominator\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 0);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(100));\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"behavior: Constraint flex apply returns full available\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.flexible(1);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 100), c.apply(100));\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(0));\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"behavior: Constraint eql checks equality\\\" {\\n+    try std.testing.expect(Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.len(10)));\\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.len(20)));\\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.minSize(10)));\\n+\\n+    try std.testing.expect(Constraint.fractional(1, 3).eql(Constraint.fractional(1, 3)));\\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.fractional(1, 3).eql(Constraint.fractional(2, 3)));\\n+}\\n+\\n+// ============================================================\\n+// REGRESSION TESTS - Edge cases\\n+// ============================================================\\n+\\n+test \\\"regression: Constraint ratio with large values doesn't overflow\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(65535, 2);\\n+    const result = c.apply(65535);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(result <= 65535);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"regression: Constraint max with zero available\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(100);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(0));\\n+}\\ndiff 100644\\nindex 0000000..ce7eb6f\\n--- /dev/null\\n+++ b/src/layout.zig\\n@@ -0,0 +1,203 @@\\n+// Layout types for zithril TUI framework\\n+// Constraint-based layout system inspired by ratatui\\n+\\n+const std = @import(\\\"std\\\");\\n+\\n+/// Direction for layout: how children are arranged.\\n+pub const Direction = enum {\\n+    horizontal,\\n+    vertical,\\n+};\\n+\\n+/// Constraints describe how space should be allocated among layout children.\\n+///\\n+/// The constraint solver allocates space in this order:\\n+/// 1. Fixed constraints (length): Allocate exact requested size\\n+/// 2. Minimum constraints (min): Allocate at least requested size\\n+/// 3. Maximum constraints (max): Allocate at most requested size\\n+/// 4. Ratio constraints (ratio): Allocate fraction of total space\\n+/// 5. Flex constraints (flex): Distribute remaining space proportionally\\n+///\\n+/// When space is insufficient:\\n+/// - Fixed/min constraints take priority\\n+/// - Flex items shrink to zero before fixed items shrink\\n+/// - No negative sizes (saturating arithmetic)\\n+pub const Constraint = union(enum) {\\n+    /// Exactly n cells.\\n+    length: u16,\\n+\\n+    /// At least n cells.\\n+    min: u16,\\n+\\n+    /// At most n cells.\\n+    max: u16,\\n+\\n+    /// Fraction of available space (numerator, denominator).\\n+    /// Example: ratio(1, 3) means 1/3 of available space.\\n+    ratio: Ratio,\\n+\\n+    /// Proportional share (like CSS flex-grow).\\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(1) = 50/50 split\\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(2) = 33/67 split\\n+    flex: u16,\\n+\\n+    pub const Ratio = struct {\\n+        num: u16,\\n+        den: u16,\\n+    };\\n+\\n+    /// Create a length constraint (exactly n cells).\\n+    pub fn len(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .length = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a minimum constraint (at least n cells).\\n+    pub fn minSize(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .min = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a maximum constraint (at most n cells).\\n+    pub fn maxSize(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .max = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a ratio constraint (num/den of available space).\\n+    pub fn fractional(num: u16, den: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .ratio = .{ .num = num, .den = den } };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Create a flex constraint (proportional share).\\n+    pub fn flexible(n: u16) Constraint {\\n+        return .{ .flex = n };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Apply this constraint to resolve a concrete size given available space.\\n+    /// Returns the size this constraint requests, which may exceed available space.\\n+    /// The caller is responsible for ensuring the total doesn't exceed available.\\n+    pub fn apply(self: Constraint, available: u16) u16 {\\n+        return switch (self) {\\n+            .length => |n| n,\\n+            .min => |n| n,\\n+            .max => |n| @min(n, available),\\n+            .ratio => |r| blk: {\\n+                if (r.den == 0) break :blk 0;\\n+                const result = (@as(u32, available) * @as(u32, r.num)) / @as(u32, r.den);\\n+                break :blk @intCast(@min(result, available));\\n+            },\\n+            .flex => available,\\n+        };\\n+    }\\n+\\n+    /// Check if two constraints are equal.\\n+    pub fn eql(self: Constraint, other: Constraint) bool {\\n+        return switch (self) {\\n+            .length => |n| other == .length and other.length == n,\\n+            .min => |n| other == .min and other.min == n,\\n+            .max => |n| other == .max and other.max == n,\\n+            .ratio => |r| other == .ratio and other.ratio.num == r.num and other.ratio.den == r.den,\\n+            .flex => |n| other == .flex and other.flex == n,\\n+        };\\n+    }\\n+};\\n+\\n+// ============================================================\\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic functionality\\n+// ============================================================\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.len creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.len(10);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .length);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), c.length);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.minSize creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.minSize(20);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .min);\\n+    try == .max);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.max);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.fractional creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 3);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .ratio);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), c.ratio.num);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 3), c.ratio.den);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Constraint.flexible creates correct constraint\\\" {\\n+    const c = Constraint.flexible(2);\\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .flex);\\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 2), c.flex);\\n+}\\n+\\n+test \\\"sanity: Direction enum values\\\" {\\n+    try std.testing.expect(@intFromEnum(Direction.horizontal) != @intFromEnum(Direction.vertical));\\n+}\\n+\\n+// Fixed constraints (length): Allocate exact requested size\n    16→/// 2. Minimum constraints (min): Allocate at least requested size\n    17→/// 3. Maximum constraints (max): Allocate at most requested size\n    18→/// 4. Ratio constraints (ratio): Allocate fraction of total space\n    19→/// 5. Flex constraints (flex): Distribute remaining space proportionally\n    20→///\n    21→/// When space is insufficient:\n    22→/// - Fixed/min constraints take priority\n    23→/// - Flex items shrink to zero before fixed items shrink\n    24→/// - No negative sizes (saturating arithmetic)\n    25→pub const Constraint = union(enum) {\n    26→    /// Exactly n cells.\n    27→    length: u16,\n    28→\n    29→    /// At least n cells.\n    30→    min: u16,\n    31→\n    32→    /// At most n cells.\n    33→    max: u16,\n    34→\n    35→    /// Fraction of available space (numerator, denominator).\n    36→    /// Example: ratio(1, 3) means 1/3 of available space.\n    37→    ratio: Ratio,\n    38→\n    39→    /// Proportional share (like CSS flex-grow).\n    40→    /// flex(1) and flex(1) = 50/50 split\n    41→    /// flex(1) and flex(2) = 33/67 split\n    42→    flex: u16,\n    43→\n    44→    pub const Ratio = struct {\n    45→        num: u16,\n    46→        den: u16,\n    47→    };\n    48→\n    49→    /// Create a length constraint (exactly n cells).\n    50→    pub fn len(n: u16) Constraint {\n    51→        return .{ .length = n };\n    52→    }\n    53→\n    54→    /// Create a minimum constraint (at least n cells).\n    55→    pub fn minSize(n: u16) Constraint {\n    56→        return .{ .min = n };\n    57→    }\n    58→\n    59→    /// Create a maximum constraint (at most n cells).\n    60→    pub fn maxSize(n: u16) Constraint {\n    61→        return .{ .max = n };\n    62→    }\n    63→\n    64→    /// Create a ratio constraint (num/den of available space).\n    65→    pub fn fractional(num: u16, den: u16) Constraint {\n    66→        return .{ .ratio = .{ .num = num, .den = den } };\n    67→    }\n    68→\n    69→    /// Create a flex constraint (proportional share).\n    70→    pub fn flexible(n: u16) Constraint {\n    71→        return .{ .flex = n };\n    72→    }\n    73→\n    74→    /// Apply this constraint to resolve a concrete size given available space.\n    75→    /// Returns the size this constraint requests, which may exceed available space.\n    76→    /// The caller is responsible for ensuring the total doesn't exceed available.\n    77→    pub fn apply(self: Constraint, available: u16) u16 {\n    78→        return switch (self) {\n    79→            .length => |n| n,\n    80→            .min => |n| n,\n    81→            .max => |n| @min(n, available),\n    82→            .ratio => |r| blk: {\n    83→                if (r.den == 0) break :blk 0;\n    84→                const result = (@as(u32, available) * r.num) / r.den;\n    85→                break :blk @intCast(@min(result, available));\n    86→            },\n    87→            .flex => available,\n    88→        };\n    89→    }\n    90→\n    91→    /// Check if two constraints are equal.\n    92→    pub fn eql(self: Constraint, other: Constraint) bool {\n    93→        return switch (self) {\n    94→            .length => |n| other == .length and other.length == n,\n    95→            .min => |n| other == .min and other.min == n,\n    96→            .max => |n| other == .max and other.max == n,\n    97→            .ratio => |r| other == .ratio and other.ratio.num == r.num and other.ratio.den == r.den,\n    98→            .flex => |n| other == .flex and other.flex == n,\n    99→        };\n   100→    }\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Maximum constraints (max): Allocate at most requested size\n/// 4. Ratio constraints (ratio): Allocate fraction of total space\n/// 5. Flex constraints (flex): Distribute remaining space proportionally\n///\n/// When space is insufficient:\n/// - Fixed/min constraints take priority\n/// - Flex items shrink to zero before fixed items shrink\n/// - No negative sizes (saturating arithmetic)\npub const Constraint = union(enum) {\n    /// Exactly n cells.\n    length: u16,\n\n    /// At least n cells.\n    min: u16,\n\n    /// At most n cells.\n    max: u16,\n\n    /// Fraction of available space (numerator, denominator).\n    /// Example: ratio(1, 3) means 1/3 of available space.\n    ratio: Ratio,\n\n    /// Proportional share (like CSS flex-grow).\n    /// flex(1) and flex(1) = 50/50 split\n    /// flex(1) and flex(2) = 33/67 split\n    flex: u16,\n\n    pub const Ratio = struct {\n        num: u16,\n        den: u16,\n    };\n\n    /// Create a length constraint (exactly n cells).\n    pub fn len(n: u16) Constraint {\n        return .{ .length = n };\n    }\n\n    /// Create a minimum constraint (at least n cells).\n n };\n    }\n\n    /// Create a ratio constraint (num/den of available space).\n    pub fn fractional(num: u16, den: u16) Constraint {\n        return .{ .ratio = .{ .num = num, .den = den } };\n    }\n\n    /// Create a flex constraint (proportional share).\n    pub fn flexible(n: u16) Constraint {\n        return .{ .flex = n };\n    }\n\n    /// Apply this constraint to resolve a concrete size given available space.\n    /// Returns the size this constraint requests, which may exceed available space.\n    /// The caller is responsible for ensuring the total doesn't exceed available.\n    pub fn apply(self: Constraint, available: u16) u16 {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .length => |n| n,\n            .min => |n| n,\n            .max => |n| @min(n, available),\n            .ratio => |r| blk: {\n                if (r.den == 0) break :blk 0;\n                const result = (@as(u32, available) * r.num) / r.den;\n                break :blk @intCast(@min(result, available));\n            },\n            .flex => available,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Check if two constraints are equal.\n    pub fn eql(self: Constraint, other: Constraint) bool {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .length => |n| other == .length and other.length == n,\n            .min => |n| other == .min and other.min == n,\n            .max => |n| other == .max and other.max == n,\n            .ratio => |r| other == .ratio and other.ratio.num == r.num and other.ratio.den == r.den,\n            .flex => |n| other == .flex and other.flex == n,\n        };\n
